aaaaabbbbcccddeimport java.util.Random;

public class Ecosystem {

	
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		Integer numNull = 0;
		Integer numBear = 0;
		Integer numFish = 0;
		
		Random rand = new Random();
		rand.setSeed(System.currentTimeMillis()); 
		
		Animal[] ecosystem = new Animal[100];
		
		
		for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++){
			switch (rand.nextInt(3)){
			case 0:
				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

}
import java.util.Random;

public class Ecosystem {

	
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		Integer numNull = 0;
		Integer numBear = 0;
		Integer numFish = 0;
		
		Random rand = new Random();
		rand.setSeed(System.currentTimeMillis()); 
		
		Animal[] ecosystem = new Animal[100];
		
		
		for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++){
			switch (rand.nextInt(3)){
			case 0:
				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

import java.util.Random;

public class Ecosystem {

	
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		Integer numNull = 0;
		Integer numBear = 0;
		Integer numFish = 0;
		
		Random rand = new Random();
		rand.setSeed(System.currentTimeMillis()); 
		
		Animal[] ecosystem = new Animal[100];
		
		
		for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++){
			switch (rand.nextInt(3)){
			case 0:
				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){

				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}

										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}

		}

public class Ecosystem {

		Random rand = new Random();

		Animal[] ecosystem = new Animal[100];
		
		
		for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++){
			switch (rand.nextInt(3)){
			case 0:
				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

}

					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}

									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");

								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

import java.util.Random;

public class Ecosystem {

	
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		Integer numNull = 0;
		Integer numBear = 0;
		Integer numFish = 0;
		
		Random rand = new Random();
		rand.setSeed(System.currentTimeMillis()); 
		
		Animal[] ecosystem = new Animal[100];
		
		
		for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++){
			switch (rand.nextInt(3)){
			case 0:
				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;

					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;

					//check for collision

					break;

					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());

import java.util.Random;

public class Ecosystem {

	
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		Integer numNull = 0;
		Integer numBear = 0;
		Integer numFish = 0;
		
		Random rand = new Random();
		rand.setSeed(System.currentTimeMillis()); 
		
		Animal[] ecosystem = new Animal[100];
		
		
		for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++){
			switch (rand.nextInt(3)){
			case 0:
				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}

		}

				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}

								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

import java.util.Random;

public class Ecosystem {

	
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		Integer numNull = 0;
		Integer numBear = 0;
		Integer numFish = 0;
		
		Random rand = new Random();
		rand.setSeed(System.currentTimeMillis()); 
		
		Animal[] ecosystem = new Animal[100];
		
		
		for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++){
			switch (rand.nextInt(3)){
			case 0:
				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

}

										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

import java.util.Random;

public class Ecosystem {

	
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		Integer numNull = 0;
		Integer numBear = 0;
		Integer numFish = 0;
		
		Random rand = new Random();
		rand.setSeed(System.currentTimeMillis()); 
		
		Animal[] ecosystem = new Animal[100];
		
		
		for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++){
			switch (rand.nextInt(3)){
			case 0:
				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;

					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;

					//check for collision

								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

import java.util.Random;

public class Ecosystem {

	
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		Integer numNull = 0;
		Integer numBear = 0;
		Integer numFish = 0;
		
		Random rand = new Random();
		rand.setSeed(System.currentTimeMillis()); 
		
		Animal[] ecosystem = new Animal[100];
		
		
		for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++){
			switch (rand.nextInt(3)){
			case 0:
				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

import java.util.Random;

public class Ecosystem {

	
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		Integer numNull = 0;
		Integer numBear = 0;
		Integer numFish = 0;
		
		Random rand = new Random();
		rand.setSeed(System.currentTimeMillis()); 
		
		Animal[] ecosystem = new Animal[100];
		
		
		for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++){
			switch (rand.nextInt(3)){
			case 0:
				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;

					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;

					//check for collision

								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

aaaaabbbbcccddeimport java.util.Random;

public class Ecosystem {

	
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		Integer numNull = 0;
		Integer numBear = 0;
		Integer numFish = 0;
		
		Random rand = new Random();
		rand.setSeed(System.currentTimeMillis()); 
		
		Animal[] ecosystem = new Animal[100];
		
		
		for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++){
			switch (rand.nextInt(3)){
			case 0:
				ecosystem[i] = new Animal();						
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
				break;
			case 1: 
				ecosystem[i] = new Bear();			
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;
			case 2:				
				ecosystem[i] = new Fish();
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());				
				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 2");
					break;					
				}
				
			}
			
			
		}		
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 100; i ++){
			if(ecosystem[i] != null){
				System.out.print(ecosystem[i].getName());
			}
		}
	
	}

				break;				
			}
		}
		
		for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++ ){
			for(int j = 0; j < 100; j++){				
				switch(rand.nextInt(3)){
				case 0://try move left
					if(j>0){
						if(ecosystem[j] != null && ecosystem[j-1] != null){							
							if(ecosystem[j].getName() == "Bear"){
								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Bear"){ //Bear + Bear makes Bear									
									//create new bear in null cell
									for(int k = 0; k < 100;k++){
										if(ecosystem[k].getName() == null){
											ecosystem[k] = new Bear();
											System.out.print("New Bear!");
											break;
										}	
									}
								}								
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == "Fish"){ //Bear + Fish makes dinner										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("FOOD!");
								}									
								if(ecosystem[j-1].getName() == null){//Bear + null, bear moves										
									ecosystem[j-1] = new Bear();
									ecosystem[j] = new Animal();
									System.out.print("New Home!");
								}
									
							}							

						}
					}					
					break;
				case 1: //try move right
					//check for collision
					//System.out.print("case 1");
					break;
				case 2: //do not move
					//check for collision

					break;

		}
